name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Friends
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Before coming, I was a little worried after reading some negative comments in the comment area. After coming, I found that there was no problem at all. From the front desk reception to the restaurant waiters to the cleaning staff, the service attitude was very good and patient. Because the return train was at 7 pm, I asked the front desk if the check-out time could be extended, and the front desk quickly coordinated it.
The room was also very comfortable, with a wide view, spacious, complete facilities, and an induction hair dryer.
The hotel has self-service flower tea, a gym, and a laundry room.
The location of the hotel looks far from the night fountain of the scenic spot, but it is actually in the new city center of Liuzhou. The infrastructure is very good. You can walk to Haiguan South Road nearby. There is a row of restaurants such as Qiushui snail noodles. It is an old store that has been opened for a long time and is a store that locals go to. It is said that many Internet celebrity stores named on Xiaohongshu now have long queues. In fact, many of them use chili essence instead of chili. I immediately have a stomachache after eating it. These small stores here make their own soup base, which is completely fine after eating.
The hotel's breakfast is rich, clean and hygienic, and is served until 10 o'clock. At 9:40, new dishes are constantly added. Generally, the hotel's buffet breakfast is almost out of food at that time. At 10 o'clock, the waiter will remind you that the meal is almost over. If you need to add any food, you can go to the food pick-up area. It is much more relaxed and comfortable to eat and drink at the hotel and then go to Qingyun Morning Market than to queue up for Internet celebrity snacks when you are hungry.
The overall experience is very good

Service: Check-in is on the top floor. From the reception downstairs to the front desk guy to the cleaning lady, they are all very enthusiastic and will take the initiative to ask the guests if they need any help. It makes up for the discomfort caused by the previous hotel.

Facilities: The room area is very generous, the design is good, there is a desk, the view is good, there is no sense of oppression at all, it is also separated from wet and dry, there is a mini bar and welcome fruit. The lighting environment is warm, the corridors are also fragrant, clean, and the comfort is full! ! There is self-service laundry, and you can also let the hotel wash it for you, which is very convenient.
The bug is the bathtub in the room, which is purely for display. If a disposable bathtub film is provided, it will not be wasted. There is also a hair dryer, the induction is not very good, and the square hand is uncomfortable to hold.

The price-performance ratio is completely OK, and many rooms include breakfast. I will also book this hotel again when I go to Liuzhou next time~
